#[HIDDEN][LOOP]Upper House Elections Check
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.130729000
	hidden = yes
	
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {	#Normal
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_SENTENCED }
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130729000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130729000.oA"
		country_event = mdmosjap_japan.130729001
	}
	
	option = {	#State Emergency Prerogative
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY_SENTENCED
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130729000.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.130729000.oB"
		country_event = mdmosjap_japan.130729002
	}
}

#[LOOP]Upper House Elections
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.130729001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.130729001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.130729001.d
	picture = GFX_eventpic_mdmosjap_jap_election
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = mdmosjap_japan.130729001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Upper House Election"
		
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { government_coalition_strength < majority_threshold }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_upper_house_election_lose_TT
			mdmosjap_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_2 = yes
		} else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_upper_house_election_win_TT
			add_political_power = 200
		}
		country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.130729000 days = 1095 }
	}
}

#[LOOP]Upper House Elections has been Suspended

#[HIDDEN]Ruling Party Check (Day after the Election Day) - TEMPORARY MEASURES
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1000
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.1000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: [HIDDEN] Ruling Party Check"
		
		# +-+-+-+-+-+-+-+ Regime Change Check Start +-+-+-+-+-+-+-+
		# ///////// Change to array^0 /////////
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 } }
					OR = {
						#Cond 1: Cannot form the LDP partisans' coalition
						has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE
						#Cond 2: Can form the LDP partisans' coalition and got votes larger than the others in the recent election
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE }
						#	check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^0 }
							check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^1 }
							check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^7 }
						}
					}
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > gov_coalition_array }
					#1 Battle Royale Check
					#	check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^0 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^1 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^2 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^3 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^4 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^5 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^6 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^7 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^8 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^9 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^10 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^11 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^12 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^13 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^14 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^15 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^16 }
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^17 }

				}
			}
			ROOT = { country_event = { hours = 1 id = mdmosjap_japanelection.10001 } }
			add_stability = -0.01
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_3 = yes
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_3 = yes
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_GOV_ADMIN_ARRAY_0
		}
		# ///////// Change to array^1 /////////
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
					OR = {
						#Cond 1: Cannot form the LDP surpartisan coalition
						has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE
						#Cond 2: Can form the LDP surpartisan coalition and got votes larger than others in the recent election
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE }
							check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^0 }
						#	check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 > party_pop_array^1 }

						}
					}
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^1 > gov_coalition_array }
					#1 Battle Royale Check
						check_variable = { party_pop_array^1 > party_pop_array^0 }

							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 8 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 9 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 10 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 11 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 12 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTMOD_ONGOING }
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 8 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 9 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 10 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 11 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 12 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTRAD_ONGOING }
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ELECTION_LOST
				country_event = { days = 3 id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3100 }
				#clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LOWER_ELECTION
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ELECTION_LOST
			}
			ROOT = {
				country_event = { days = 3 id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3101 }
				#clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LOWER_ELECTION
			}
		}
	}
}

				name = "Nobuteru Ishihara"
				picture = "Nobuteru_Ishihara.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					rational
					humble
					narcissist
					geopolitical_thinker
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
				has_country_leader = { name = "Shinjiro Koizumi" }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shinjiro Koizumi"
				picture = "Shinjiro_Koizumi.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					cautious
					stubborn
					narcissist
					inexperienced
					likeable
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
				has_country_leader = { name = "Yoshihide Suga" }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yoshihide Suga"
				picture = "yoshihide_suga.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					cautious
					stubborn
					mediafuror
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		
		#Trait Load
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1 }
			add_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer1
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2 }
			add_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer2
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2
		}
	}
}

#Election Event: Initial Event, Based on Original Millennium Dawn
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1100
	title = MD4_election_campaign.0.t
	desc = MD4_election_campaign.0.d
	picture = GFX_election_day
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		display_election_campaign_status = yes
		campaign_spending_initial = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = MD4_election_campaign.0.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.1100 - Executed"
		country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.1 days = 2 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1900 days = 14 }
	#		country_event = { id = MD4_election.0 days = 14 }				#Call Original Event
			#controversial speaker event
	#		if = {
	#			limit = {
	#				check_variable = { government_coalition_strength < majority_threshold }
	#			}
	#			random_list = {
	#				35 = { }
	#				65 = { country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.8 days = 8 } }
	#			}
	#		}
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = gov_coalition_array
			value = v
			multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^v = ads_budget_effect?1 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ruling_party
			value = v
			multiply_variable = { party_pop_array^v = ads_budget_effect?1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			recalculate_party = yes
			clear_variable = ads_budget_effect
		}
	}
}

#Choose the next Prime Minister - Array 0 (The LDP Pro US Conservative Lineage)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1800
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.1800.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.1800.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
#	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
		#	clear_array = gov_coalition_array
		#	remove_mission = coalition_countdown
			
			### Add the LDP Tripartisan Coalition ###
			if = {
				### Condition ###
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE }
				}
				
				### Trigger ###
				#Trait Save
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer1 }
					set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer2 }

					limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = uyoku_supporter }

					limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = sayoku_supporter }
					set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = conservative_lib }
					set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB
				}
				
				#westaut
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westcon_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_emeraut_TT
				}
				#westcon
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
						
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westaut_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_emeraut_TT
				}
				#thirdcon
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westaut_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westcon_TT
				}
			}
		
			clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
		}
	}

					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_MASAYOSHI_TAKEMURA
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RETIREMENT_MASAYOSHI_TAKEMURA }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_MASAYOSHI_TAKEMURA }

#[HIDDEN] Election Event: Election Result Calculation, Based on Original Millennium Dawn
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1900
	title = MD4_election.0.t
	desc = MD4_election.0.d
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { recalculate_party = yes update_government_coalition_strength = yes update_party_name = yes set_coalition_drift = yes }
		clr_country_flag = campaign_funding_count
		election_mdmosjap_JAP_update_next_election_date = yes
		hold_elections = yes
		#any single party is over election threshold - set them to rule immediately
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { party_pop_array^max_index_1 > majority_threshold }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = max_index_1 }
			}
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1901 }		#The Ruling Wins Alone then Do the LDP Tripartisan Coalition Check
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { party_pop_array^max_index_1 > majority_threshold }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = max_index_1 } }
			}
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1004 }		#Check Scenario then Elect Another Party Alone
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect > majority_threshold }
			}
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1902 }		#The Coalition Wins
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect > majority_threshold } }
				check_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect > party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^0 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^1 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^2 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^3 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^4 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^5 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^6 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^7 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 8 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^8 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 9 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^9 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 10 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^10 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 11 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^11 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 12 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^12 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^13 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^14 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^15 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^16 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^17 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^18 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^19 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^20 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^21 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^22 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
				} else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 } } check_variable = { party_pop_array^23 < party_pop_array^max_index_1 } }
			#	NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = max_index_1 }
				is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = max_index_1 } 
			}
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1953 }		#The Coalition Leader Swapped
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect > majority_threshold } }
				check_variable = { government_coalition_strength_elect > party_pop_array^max_index_1 }
			#	is_in_array = { ruling_party = max_index_1 }
			}
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1952 }		#The Coalition Wins, By a Narrow
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				date > 2030.1.1
			}
			AI_setup_government = yes
			
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
			#	is_ai = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { ruling_party_strength = 0 }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = ruling_party
				value = v
				add_to_temp_variable = { ruling_party_strength = party_pop_elect_array^v }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
			#		is_ai = no 
					check_variable = { ruling_party_strength < election_threshold }
				}
				country_event = { id = MD4_election.5 }		#Embarrassing Defeat, Cede the Seat to 1st Winner or 2nd Winner
			} else_if = {
			#	country_event = { id = MD4_election.4 }		#Inconclusive Outcome, Try to Re-Form a New Coalition
				country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1004 }	#Or Just Lose
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_North_America = yes
					is_major = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_North_America = yes is_ai = no }
					news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_South_America = yes
					is_major = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_South_America = yes is_ai = no }
					news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_middle_eastern_nation = yes
					is_major = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_middle_eastern_nation = yes is_ai = no }
					news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_african_nation = yes
					is_major = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_african_nation = yes is_ai = no }
					news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					 is_european_nation = yes
					is_major = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_european_nation = yes is_ai = no }
					news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_asian_nation = yes
					is_major = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_asian_nation = yes is_ai = no }
					news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_oceania_nation = yes
					is_major = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_oceania_nation = yes is_ai = no }
					news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_major = yes
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_ai = no }
					news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.1 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		election_mdmosjap_JAP_clear_date_of_election_relative_events = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = MD4_election.0.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.1900 - executed"
	}
}

#Election Event: Single Party Wins Election, Based on Original Millennium Dawn
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1901
	title = MD4_election.1.t
	desc = MD4_election.1.d
	picture = GFX_election_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_array = gov_coalition_array
		#	remove_mission = coalition_countdown
			
			### [KATO] Execute LDP Kochikai's Coalition Invitation to DPJ ###
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } }
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_EPILOGUE_KONO_ENDING_COALITION_WITH_DPJ
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_LDP_DPJ_COALITION_YES
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RIKKEN }
				}
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_LDP_DPJ_COALITION_YES
			#	remove_mission = coalition_countdown
			#	clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
			}
			
			### Add the LDP Tripartisan Coalition ###
			if = {
				### Condition ###
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE }
				}
				
				#westaut
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westcon_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_emeraut_TT
				}
				#westcon
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
						
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westaut_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_emeraut_TT
				}
				#thirdcon
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westaut_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westcon_TT
				}
				remove_mission = coalition_countdown
				clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
			}
			
			### Trait Save ###
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer1 }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer2 }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = uyoku_supporter }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = sayoku_supporter }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = conservative_lib }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB
			}
				
		#	clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = MD4_election.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.1901 - Executed"
		add_political_power = 150
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { news_event = { days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 } } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_North_America = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_North_America = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_South_America = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_South_America = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_middle_eastern_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_middle_eastern_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_african_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_african_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				 is_european_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_european_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_asian_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_asian_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_oceania_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_oceania_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_major = yes
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
	}

#Election Event: Coalition Victory, Based on Original Millennium Dawn
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1902
	title = MD4_election.2.t
	desc = MD4_election.2.d
	picture = GFX_election_rally
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_array = gov_coalition_array
		#	remove_mission = coalition_countdown
			
			### [KATO] Execute LDP Kochikai's Coalition Invitation to DPJ ###
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } }
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_EPILOGUE_KONO_ENDING_COALITION_WITH_DPJ
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_LDP_DPJ_COALITION_YES
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RIKKEN }
				}
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_LDP_DPJ_COALITION_YES
			#	remove_mission = coalition_countdown
			#	clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
			}
			
			### Add the LDP Tripartisan Coalition ###
			if = {
				### Condition ###
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE }
				}
				
				#westaut
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westcon_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_emeraut_TT
				}
				#westcon
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
						
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westaut_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_emeraut_TT
				}
				#thirdcon
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westaut_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westcon_TT
				}
				remove_mission = coalition_countdown
				clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
			}
			
			### Trait Save ###
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer1 }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer2 }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = uyoku_supporter }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = sayoku_supporter }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = conservative_lib }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB
			}
				
		#	clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = MD4_election.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.1902.oA"
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { news_event = { days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 } } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_North_America = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_North_America = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_South_America = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_South_America = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_middle_eastern_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_middle_eastern_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_african_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_african_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				 is_european_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_european_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_asian_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_asian_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_oceania_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_oceania_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_major = yes
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.0 }
			}
		}

	}
	option = {
		name = MD4_election.2.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.1902.oB"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		clear_array = gov_coalition_array
		hidden_effect = { recalculate_party = yes }
		#trigger mission desicion
		set_country_flag = coalition_forming
		activate_mission = coalition_countdown
	}
}

#Election Event: Another Party Wins, Based on Original Millennium Dawn
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1903
	title = MD4_election.3.t
	desc = MD4_election.3.d
	picture = GFX_election_day

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_array = gov_coalition_array
			remove_mission = coalition_countdown
			
			### Add the LDP Tripartisan Coalition ###
			if = {
				### Condition ###
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE }
				}
				
				### Trigger ###
				#Trait Save
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer1 }
					set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer2 }
					clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
					set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = uyoku_supporter }
					set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = sayoku_supporter }
					set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = conservative_lib }
					set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB
				}
				
				#westaut
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westcon_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_emeraut_TT
				}
				#westcon
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
						
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westaut_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_emeraut_TT
				}
				#thirdcon
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westaut_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westcon_TT
				}
			}
		
			clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = MD4_election.3.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.1903.oA"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
		changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_addflag_resignation = yes			#Make a flag for the resignation of former P.M.
		
		clear_array = ruling_party
		clear_array = gov_coalition_array
		add_to_array = { ruling_party = max_index_1 }
		hidden_effect = { recalculate_party = yes }
		#switch to ruling
		hidden_effect = {
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_country_flag = [META_SET_RULING_PARTY]
				}
				META_SET_RULING_PARTY = "[meta_set_ruling_leader]"
			}
			set_leader = yes
		}
		
		hidden_effect = { remove_mission = coalition_countdown }
		
		hidden_effect = { ROOT = { news_event = { days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.2 } } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_North_America = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_North_America = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_South_America = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_South_America = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_middle_eastern_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_middle_eastern_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_african_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_african_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				 is_european_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_european_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_asian_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_asian_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_oceania_nation = yes
				is_major = no
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_oceania_nation = yes is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_major = yes
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {  days = 1 id = News_MD4_election.2 }
			}
		}
		
		changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_prime_minister_election = yes		#Choose the next Prime Minister
	}
}

#Election Event: Coalition Victory But Leader Swapped
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1953
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.1953.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.1953.d
	picture = GFX_election_rally
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
		#	clear_array = gov_coalition_array
		#	remove_mission = coalition_countdown
			
			### [KATO] Execute LDP Kochikai's Coalition Invitation to DPJ ###
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } }
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_EPILOGUE_KONO_ENDING_COALITION_WITH_DPJ
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_LDP_DPJ_COALITION_YES
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RIKKEN }
				}
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_LDP_DPJ_COALITION_YES
			#	remove_mission = coalition_countdown
			#	clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
			}
			
			### Add the LDP Tripartisan Coalition ###
			if = {
				### Condition ###
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
								NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE }
				}
				
				#westaut
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westcon_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_emeraut_TT
				}
				#westcon
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
						
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westaut_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_emeraut_TT
				}
				#thirdcon
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 0 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westaut_TT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } }
					}
					add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_coalition_westcon_TT
				}
				remove_mission = coalition_countdown
				clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
			}
			
			### Trait Save ###
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer1 }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer2 }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = uyoku_supporter }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = sayoku_supporter }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = conservative_lib }
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB
			}
				
		#	clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
		}
	}

#Regime Change: array^0
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.10001
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.10001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.10001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		JAP = {
			clear_array = ruling_party
			clear_array = gov_coalition_array
			add_to_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
			
			clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
			hidden_effect = { remove_mission = coalition_countdown }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.10001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.10001.oA"
		#Mori Yoshiro (Before Ehimemaru or Quit Golf)
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_MORI_RESIGNED }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_PROGOLFER_MORI }
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yoshiro Mori"
				picture = "yoshiro_mori.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					stubborn
					narcissist
				}
			}
		}
		#Mori Yoshiro (After Ehimemaru and Played Golf)
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_MORI_RESIGNED }
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_PROGOLFER_MORI
					NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Junichiro Koizumi" } }		#For flag error
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yoshiro Mori"
				picture = "yoshiro_mori.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					stubborn
					narcissist
					incapable
				}
			}
		}
		
		### PUT KATO HERE IF THE CONCEPTION OF AN ALTERNATIVE HISTORY HAS JELLED
		
		#Koizumi Junichiro
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_MORI_RESIGNED
						NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KOIZUMI_RESIGNED }
					}
					has_country_leader = { name = "Junichiro Koizumi" }		#For flag error
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Junichiro Koizumi"
				picture = "junichiro_koizumi.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					stubborn
				#	austerity_economics
					mediafuror
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		#Shinzo Abe (First Time)
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KOIZUMI_RESIGNED
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ABE_RESIGNED_I }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shinzo Abe"
				picture = "Shinzo_Abe.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					zealous
					stubborn
					wgip
					antikorea
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		#Yasuo Fukuda
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ABE_RESIGNED_I
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_FUKUDA_RESIGNED }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yasuo Fukuda"
				picture = "yasuo_fukuda.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					rational
					cautious
					humble
					pro_china
					conservative_lib
				}
			}
		}
		#Taro Aso
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_FUKUDA_RESIGNED
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ASO_RESIGNED }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Taro Aso"
				picture = "taro_aso.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					rash
					stubborn
					narcissist
					polished
					likeable
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		
		### PUT ADDITIONAL LEADERS HERE IF THE CONCEPTION OF AN ALTERNATIVE HISTORY ABOUT WHAT IF LDP WON THE 2009 LOWER HOUSE ELECTION HAS JELLED
		### e.g. SADAKAZU TANIGAKI, SHIGERU ISHIBA, TARO ASO, SHINJIRO KOIZUMI, etc
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TANIGAKI_RESIGNED }
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ISHIBA_RESIGNED }
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_MACHIMURA_RESIGNED }
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ISHIHARA_RESIGNED }
		
		#Shinzo Abe (Second Time)
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ASO_RESIGNED
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_2012_LDP_PRESIDENT_ABE
				
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shinzo Abe"
				picture = "Shinzo_Abe.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					zealous
					stubborn
					wgip
					antikorea
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		#Shigeru Ishiba
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ASO_RESIGNED
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_2012_LDP_PRESIDENT_ISHIBA
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shigeru Ishiba"
				picture = "Shigeru_Ishiba.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					cautious
					stubborn
					likeable
					capable
					military_genius
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		#Nobuteru Ishihara
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ASO_RESIGNED
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_2012_LDP_PRESIDENT_ISHIHARA
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Nobuteru Ishihara"
				picture = "Nobuteru_Ishihara.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					rational
					humble
					narcissist
					geopolitical_thinker
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		news_event = { id = News_MD4_election.2 days = 1 }
		
		#Trait Load
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1 }
			add_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer1
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2 }
			add_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer2
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO }
			add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO }
			add_country_leader_trait = sayoku_supporter
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB }
			add_country_leader_trait = conservative_lib
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB
		}
	}

#Regime Change: array^1
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.10101
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.10101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.10101.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		JAP = {
			clear_array = ruling_party
			clear_array = gov_coalition_array
			add_to_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
			
			clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
			hidden_effect = { remove_mission = coalition_countdown }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.10101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.10101.oA"
		#Mori Yoshiro (Before Ehimemaru or Quit Golf)
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_MORI_RESIGNED }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_PROGOLFER_MORI }
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yoshiro Mori"
				picture = "yoshiro_mori.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					stubborn
					narcissist
				}
			}
		}
		#Mori Yoshiro (After Ehimemaru and Played Golf)
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_MORI_RESIGNED }
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_PROGOLFER
					NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Junichiro Koizumi" } }		#For flag error
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yoshiro Mori"
				picture = "yoshiro_mori.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					stubborn
					narcissist
					incapable
				}
			}
		}
		
		### PUT KATO HERE IF THE CONCEPTION OF AN ALTERNATIVE HISTORY HAS JELLED
		
		#Koizumi Junichiro
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_MORI_RESIGNED
						NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KOIZUMI_RESIGNED }
					}
					has_country_leader = { name = "Junichiro Koizumi" }		#For flag error
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Junichiro Koizumi"
				picture = "junichiro_koizumi.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					stubborn
				#	austerity_economics
					mediafuror
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		#Shinzo Abe (First Time)
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KOIZUMI_RESIGNED
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ABE_RESIGNED_I }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shinzo Abe"
				picture = "Shinzo_Abe.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					zealous
					stubborn
					wgip
					antikorea
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		#Yasuo Fukuda
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ABE_RESIGNED_I
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_FUKUDA_RESIGNED }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yasuo Fukuda"
				picture = "yasuo_fukuda.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					rational
					cautious
					humble
					pro_china
					conservative_lib
				}
			}
		}
		#Taro Aso
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_FUKUDA_RESIGNED
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ASO_RESIGNED }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Taro Aso"
				picture = "taro_aso.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					rash
					stubborn
					narcissist
					polished
					likeable
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		
		### PUT ADDITIONAL LEADERS HERE IF THE CONCEPTION OF AN ALTERNATIVE HISTORY ABOUT WHAT IF LDP WON THE 2009 LOWER HOUSE ELECTION HAS JELLED
		### e.g. SADAKAZU TANIGAKI, SHIGERU ISHIBA, TARO ASO, SHINJIRO KOIZUMI, etc
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TANIGAKI_RESIGNED }
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ISHIBA_RESIGNED }
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_MACHIMURA_RESIGNED }
				#NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ISHIHARA_RESIGNED }
		
		#Shinzo Abe (Second Time)
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ASO_RESIGNED
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_2012_LDP_PRESIDENT_ABE
				
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shinzo Abe"
				picture = "Shinzo_Abe.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					emotional
					zealous
					stubborn
					wgip
					antikorea
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		#Shigeru Ishiba
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ASO_RESIGNED
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_2012_LDP_PRESIDENT_ISHIBA
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Shigeru Ishiba"
				picture = "Shigeru_Ishiba.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					cautious
					stubborn
					likeable
					capable
					military_genius
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		#Nobuteru Ishihara
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ASO_RESIGNED
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_2012_LDP_PRESIDENT_ISHIHARA
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Nobuteru Ishihara"
				picture = "Nobuteru_Ishihara.dds"
				ideology = conservatism
				traits = {
					western_conservatism
					rational
					humble
					narcissist
					geopolitical_thinker
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		news_event = { id = News_MD4_election.2 days = 1 }
		
		#Trait Load
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1 }
			add_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer1
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2 }
			add_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer2
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO }
			add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO }
			add_country_leader_trait = sayoku_supporter
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB }
			add_country_leader_trait = conservative_lib
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB
		}
	}
}

#Regime Change: array^2
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.10201
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.10201.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.10201.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		JAP = {
			clear_array = ruling_party
			clear_array = gov_coalition_array
			add_to_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
			
			clr_country_flag = coalition_forming
			hidden_effect = { remove_mission = coalition_countdown }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.10201.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.10201.oA"
		#Yukio Hatoyama
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_WESTLIB_NAOTO_KAN }
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_WESTLIB_YUKIO_HATOYAMA
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yukio Hatoyama"
				picture = "yukio_hatoyama.dds"
				ideology = liberalism
				traits = {
					western_liberalism
					stubborn
					polished
					inexperienced
					pro_china
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = sayoku_supporter
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_WESTLIB_NAOTO_KAN
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_WESTLIB_YUKIO_HATOYAMA }
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Naoto Kan"
				picture = "naoto_kan.dds"
				ideology = liberalism
				traits = {
					western_liberalism
					emotional
					stubborn
					tech_savy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = sayoku_supporter
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KAN_RESIGNED
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yoshihiko Noda"
				picture = "yoshihiko_noda.dds"
				ideology = liberalism
				traits = {
					western_liberalism
					humble
					political_dancer
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NODA_RESIGNED
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_DPJ_SURVIVED
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Banri Kaieda"
				picture = "Banri_Kaieda.dds"
				ideology = liberalism
				traits = {
					western_liberalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = sayoku_supporter
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NODA_RESIGNED
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_DPJ_SURVIVED
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Ichiro Ozawa"
				picture = "ichiro_ozawa.dds"
				ideology = liberalism
				traits = {
					western_liberalism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
				add_country_leader_trait = sayoku_supporter
			}
		}
		news_event = { id = News_MD4_election.2 days = 1 }
		
		#Trait Load
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1 }
			add_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer1
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2 }
			add_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer2
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO }
			add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO }
			add_country_leader_trait = sayoku_supporter
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB }
			add_country_leader_trait = conservative_lib
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB
		}
	}
}

				name = "Takako Doi"
				picture = "takako_doi.dds"
				ideology = socialism
				traits = {
					western_socialism
				}
			}
		}

			limit = {

				picture = "mizuho_fukushima.dds"

			add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_UYO
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO }

			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_SAYO
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB }
			add_country_leader_trait = conservative_lib
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_CONSERVATIVE_LIB
		}
		
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LOWER_ELECTION
	}
}

#Revisionists: \"Launch the Referendum of Constitutional Amendment\"
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.2002
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.2002.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.2002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#It's a bit too early to do...
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }
				factor = 0.2
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					}
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					date > 2021.1.0
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.2002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.2002.oA"
		decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_2 = yes
		add_political_power = -100
	}
	
	#... It's time to make a epic move.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					date < 2021.1.0
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.2002.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.2002.oB"
		#increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_10 = yes
		add_stability = -0.05
		activate_mission = mdmosjap_JAP_the_great_referendum
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3001 days = 1 }	#The Party's Supportive Draft on the Amendment
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION }
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LOWER_ELECTION
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3004 days = 2 }	#Grand Coalition for the Amendment
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_JAPAN_EXPERIENCED_FIRST_TIME_REFERENDUM } }
			news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.2002
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_ONGOING
		set_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_JAPAN_EXPERIENCED_FIRST_TIME_REFERENDUM
	}
}

	id = mdmosjap_japannews.2002
	title = mdmosjap_japannews.2002.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japannews.2002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes

	#Japan
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.2002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.2002.oA"
	}
	
	#Asia
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.2002.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.2002.oB"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = australia }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = north_america }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = south_america }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.2002.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.2002.oC"
	}
}

		mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_18_var_8 = yes

			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3003 hours = 12 }
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTMOD_ONGOING
	}
	
	#We will install revolutionaly draft without any revolution! [LEFTIST OPTION - FAR]
	option = {

			}

#A Proposal of Grand Coalition toward the Amendment
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3004
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.3004.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.3004.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#A golden opportunity! Let's call to form the coalition!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		#	modifier = {
		#		check_variable = { government_coalition_strength > 0.666 }
		#		factor = 0
		#	}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3004.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3004.oA"
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_enable_form_grand_coalition_TT
		ROOT = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION }
		country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3006 days = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			recalculate_party = yes
			update_government_coalition_strength = yes
			update_party_name = yes
			set_coalition_drift = yes
		}
	}
	
	#Nah, our coalition is big enough.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { government_coalition_strength < 0.666 }
					check_variable = { government_coalition_strength = 0.666 }
					
					#RIGHT: LDP-JIP-DPFP TIE
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
					
					#LEFT: CDP-SDP-JCP TIE
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					
					#TIMEOUT BY PLAYER
					is_ai = no
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3004.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3004.oB"
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_3 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_coalition_party_popularity_3 = yes
		add_stability = 0.03
		add_political_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTMOD_ONGOING
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTRAD_ONGOING
				}
			}
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_1 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTMOD_ONGOING
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTRAD_ONGOING
				}
			}
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3006 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Budget Using in the Newspaper Advertising
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3006
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.3006.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.3006.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#No advertising on newspapers
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3006.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3006.oA"
		decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3007 days = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ADVERTISING_NEWSPAPER_LESS
	}
	
	#Bottom of a page
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 9
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3006.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3006.oB"
		add_political_power = -100
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_coalition_party_popularity_1 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3007 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	#Occupy two pages
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3006.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3006.oC"
		add_political_power = -200
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_4 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_coalition_party_popularity_2 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3007 days = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ADVERTISING_NEWSPAPER_MUCH
	}
}

#Budget Using in the Broadcast
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3007
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.3007.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.3007.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#30 seconds of commercial messages
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3007.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3007.oA"
		decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3008 days = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ADVERTISING_BROADCAST_LESS
	}
	
	#2 minutes commercial announcement
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 9
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3007.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3007.oB"
		add_political_power = -100
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_coalition_party_popularity_1 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3008 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	#\"Dispatch the commentator\" in every news program.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3007.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3007.oC"
		add_political_power = -200
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_4 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_4 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_coalition_party_popularity_2 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3008 days = 1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ADVERTISING_BROADCAST_MUCH
	}
}

#Counter Advertising by Protectionists
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3009
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.3009.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.3009.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3009.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3009.oA"
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { government_coalition_strength < 0.333 }
					check_variable = { government_coalition_strength = 0.333 }
				}
			}
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_10 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { government_coalition_strength > 0.334 }
					check_variable = { government_coalition_strength = 0.334 }
					check_variable = { government_coalition_strength < 0.666 }
					check_variable = { government_coalition_strength = 0.666 }
				}
			}
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_7 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { government_coalition_strength > 0.667 }
					check_variable = { government_coalition_strength = 0.667 }
				}
			}
			increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_4 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_3 = yes
		}
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_2 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION }
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ADVERTISING_NEWSPAPER_LESS
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ADVERTISING_BROADCAST_LESS
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ADVERTISING_INTERNET_LESS
			}
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3010 days = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION }
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ADVERTISING_NEWSPAPER_MUCH
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ADVERTISING_BROADCAST_MUCH
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_ADVERTISING_INTERNET_MUCH
			}
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3011 days = 3 }
		}
	}

			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3102 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}
