#The Day of Referendum
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3201
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.3201.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.3201.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#immediate = { ROOT = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_THE_GREAT_REFERENDUM_MALCONCLUSION } }
	
	#The amendment has been approved by the nation
	option = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightCon > 50 } }
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3201.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3201.oA"
		add_stability = 0.03
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_REVISE_APPROVED
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTMOD_ONGOING
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTMOD_ONGOING
				}
			}
			add_named_threat = { threat = 1.0 name = MDMOSJAP_referendum_approved_moderate_amendment }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTRAD_ONGOING
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTRAD_ONGOING
				}
			}
			add_named_threat = { threat = 2.0 name = MDMOSJAP_referendum_approved_radical_amendment }
		}
		country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3202 days = 1 }		#Protectionists growling about the procedure of referendum
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3205 months = 6 }		#[HIDDEN]Amendment Deadline: First AFK Check
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_AMENDMENT_DEADLINE_TICKING
		complete_national_focus = JAP_amendment_election
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.3202
	}
	
	#The amendment has been rejected by the nation
	option = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightCon < 50 } }
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3201.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3201.oB"
		add_stability = 0.03
		#set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_REVISE_REJECTED
		decrease_mdmosjap_concon_right_10 = yes
		country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3302 days = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTMOD_ONGOING }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTMOD_ONGOING
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTRAD_ONGOING }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTRAD_ONGOING
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTMOD_ONGOING }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTMOD_ONGOING
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTRAD_ONGOING }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTRAD_ONGOING
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTMOD_DIDNT_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTMOD_DIDNT_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTRAD_DIDNT_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTRAD_DIDNT_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTMOD_DIDNT_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTMOD_DIDNT_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTRAD_DIDNT_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTRAD_DIDNT_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTMOD_MAKES_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTMOD_MAKES_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTRAD_MAKES_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTRAD_MAKES_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTMOD_MAKES_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTMOD_MAKES_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTRAD_MAKES_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTRAD_MAKES_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_SGI_MEMBERS_ANTAGONISING_AMENDMENT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_SGI_MEMBERS_ANTAGONISING_AMENDMENT
		}
		removeflag_mdmosjap_coalition_invitation = yes
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.3302
	}
	
	#The vote was tie; The amendment has been rejected.
	option = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightCon = 50 } }
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3201.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3201.oC"
		add_stability = 0.03
		#set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_REVISE_REJECTED
		decrease_mdmosjap_concon_right_5 = yes
		country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3302 days = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTMOD_ONGOING }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTMOD_ONGOING
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTRAD_ONGOING }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTRAD_ONGOING
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTMOD_ONGOING }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTMOD_ONGOING
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTRAD_ONGOING }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTRAD_ONGOING
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTMOD_DIDNT_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTMOD_DIDNT_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTRAD_DIDNT_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTRAD_DIDNT_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTMOD_DIDNT_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTMOD_DIDNT_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTRAD_DIDNT_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTRAD_DIDNT_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTMOD_MAKES_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTMOD_MAKES_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTRAD_MAKES_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_LEFTRAD_MAKES_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTMOD_MAKES_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTMOD_MAKES_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTRAD_MAKES_EFFORT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_FIRSTTIME_RIGHTRAD_MAKES_EFFORT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_SGI_MEMBERS_ANTAGONISING_AMENDMENT }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_SGI_MEMBERS_ANTAGONISING_AMENDMENT
		}
		removeflag_mdmosjap_coalition_invitation = yes
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.3302
	}
}

#Japan's Referendum Approved the Constitutional Amendment
news_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japannews.3202
	title = mdmosjap_japannews.3202.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japannews.3202.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes

	#Japan
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.3202.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.3202.oA"
	}
	
	#Asia - Moderate Amendment
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTMOD_ONGOING
						has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTMOD_ONGOING
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.3202.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.3202.oB"
	}
	
	#Asia - Radical Left Amendment
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
				JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_LEFTRAD_ONGOING }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.3202.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.3202.oC"
	}
	
	#Asia - Radical Right Amendment
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
				JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_RIGHTRAD_ONGOING }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.3202.oD
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.3202.oD"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = australia }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = north_america }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = south_america }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.3202.oE
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.3202.oE"
	}
}

#Protectionists growling about the procedure of referendum
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3202
	title = mdmosjap_japanelection.3202.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japanelection.3202.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Ignore them
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3202.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3202.oA"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_political_power = -80
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3203 days = 7 }
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_INSPECTION_IGNORED_BIG
	}
	
	#Inspect the result with the coalition
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3202.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3202.oB"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -160
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3204 days = 7 }
		}
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_INSPECTION_IGNORED_SMALL
	}
	
	#Inspect the result with Protectionists and outsiders

#[HIDDEN]Amendment Deadline: First AFK Check
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japanelection.3205
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Nothing in 6 months -> first complaint
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_HOLY_ARTICLE_9 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ADAPT_ARTICLE_9 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ADAPT_STATE_EMERGENCY_PREROGATIVE }
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_AMENDMENT_DEADLINE_TICKING
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3205.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3205.oA"
		country_event = mdmosjap_japanelection.3206
	}
	
	#Nothing in 12 months -> second complaint
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_HOLY_ARTICLE_9 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ADAPT_ARTICLE_9 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ADAPT_STATE_EMERGENCY_PREROGATIVE }
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_AMENDMENT_DEADLINE_TICKING2
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3205.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3205.oB"
		country_event = mdmosjap_japanelection.3207
	}
	
	#Nothing in 18 months -> final complaint
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_HOLY_ARTICLE_9 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ADAPT_ARTICLE_9 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ADAPT_STATE_EMERGENCY_PREROGATIVE }
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_AMENDMENT_DEADLINE_TICKING3
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3205.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3205.oC"
		country_event = mdmosjap_japanelection.3208
	}
	
	#End Recalculation
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_AMENDMENT_DEADLINE_TICKING }
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_HOLY_ARTICLE_9
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ADAPT_ARTICLE_9
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ADAPT_STATE_EMERGENCY_PREROGATIVE
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japanelection.3205.EndLoop
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japanelection.3205.EndLoop"
	}
}

				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = australia }
